1a5(tog gzungs): gang gis mkhyen pa'i 'od kyis 'gro ba'i mu la sel zhing / sprin kro la lam gyi rnam mkhyen se la 'gong mdzad pa'i/ rab gnas mkhan po bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ k+She/ 'dzam bu gling dbus rdo ga dar gyi byang // brdal ba bkong li gso rin chems bzhi'i sdeng
1a6(tog gzungs): dam chos dar+ya ba 'dzam gling sogs khwa'i dbus// khA ba can ljongs sta n+ya bo da ra ba'i sa// lha gnas mi lu 'phos 'dra'i rgyalnga sa smon thang deraHbstan pa'i ga nau dang rgyal ba byams pa dang // bka' 'gyur bstan 'gyur gser gI ge pa zhugs// de'i sbyin
1a7(tog gzungs): bdag chen por gyur pa ni/ mi dbang chen po rgya ho re dza ba liM bza pa phyogs las rgyal gyur cig/ k+Shi / ba de'i chab skyid legs sbyangs pa'i mang 'a// yul la ga yang chags ta ra ba zhes bya drer po sa la 'bur do de kr-i so na 'gro zhes nyid du/ 
1a8(tog gzungs): mi rigs bzang po pha chen ga rtsa 'khor rgyu // bslab gsum nam ngag tshul khrims rgyan gyis spras/ mdo rgyud rgya 'tsho'i tshogs la logs sbyangs pa'i/ dge slong rgyal mtshan seng ge zhes bya ba stod/ dri med tshul khrims chu bya nyim legs par sbas
1a9(tog gzungs): dpon btsun seng ge skyab pa zhes nyid de stong // skyes pa'i pho la grags pa'i snyan pa can/ 'dzangs rlung ldan pas nye 'brel kun dang 'thun// yon gyi bdag po bu chung 'phan dar zhes ji bsto / byi sho'i cha rnam 'phrul rig byed 'khan// 
1a10(tog gzungs): dpor btsun dbang phyuka don yod khye la bstod// gzhon nu rab byung tshul khrimasde chab gyis gang // dag shes bsam 'phel bzang po bya ba lags// rig pa'i rnam 'phrul rig bye du 'a khA me/ phung po'i mchog gyur dpon chen sher+ya bzang khyed la bstod

11b1(tog gzungs): ldan 'das kyi gzi brjid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus skyes bu dam pa de gnyis kyis ri de yang ma mthong / seng ge de yang ma mthong / seng ge'i skad kyang ma thos te/ lam drang por/ 
11b2(tog gzungs): bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de ru logasu song ngo // bcom ldan 'das ni 'khor mang po brgya stong du mas yongs su bskor cing mdun gyis bltas nas chos ston te/ de nas bcom ldan
11b3(tog gzungs): 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' bskal pa/ dge slong dag khyed skyes bu dam pa tshogs kyi gtso bo g.yog gi tshegs can 'di gnyis la bltos/ de dag gis gsol pa/ bcos
11b4(tog gzungs): ldan 'das mthong lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyi sa bka' stsal pa/ dge slong dag skyes bu pa khyad pa 'di gnyis g.yog dang bcas te nga'i thad du rab tu byung nas/ gcig/ 
11b5(tog gzungs): ni nga'i nyan thos thams cad kyi nang na shes rab can gyi mchog tu 'gyur ro// gcig ni rdzu 'phrul can gyi mchog tu 'gyur ro// de nas dge slong zhig gis/ de'i tshe tshigs
11b6(tog gzungs): su bcad pa 'di smras so// skyes bu mkhas pa g.yog ldan 'di gnyis ni/ rdzu 'phrul ldan drang shes rab 'jigs med par/ mi mchog phan par mdzad pas lung bstan te/ bdag
11b7(tog gzungs): gis de gnyis bsti bstang bskyed nas bsu/ de nas dge slong de stan las langs te/ dge slong mang po dang / khyim na gnas pa dang / rab tu byung ba mang po dang lhan cig tu// 
12a1(tog gzungs): skyes bu dam pa de gnyis bsu nas bsnyen bkur byaso// de nas skyes bu dam pa de gnas bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das
12a2(tog gzungs): kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyog 'tshal te/ len gsum bskor ba byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'dug ste/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan
12a3(tog gzungs): 'das rab tu byung ba dang / bsnyen par rdzogs par dge sbyong gi dngos po bdag cag gnyis la bskul du gsol/ bdag cag bcom ldan 'das kyi thad du tshangs par spyad pa/ 
12a4(tog gzungs): spyod do// ma ldan 'odas kyis bka/ 'a bsgral pa'ikyi bu khyed gnyis kyi ming ni ci/ rgyal gyis gsol pa/ bdag ni bram ze zhe rgyal gyi bu lags ni ni
12a5(tog gzungs): rgyal zhes bgyi/ bdag gi ma'i ming ni shA ri kA ste/ bde ga de las skyes pas na de'i slad du bdage gI mA ni shA ra'i bu zhes btags so// bdag rab tu byung yang pha mas
12a6(tog gzungs): gnang lagres so// bong nas kyis gsol pa/ bdag gi bya'i ming ni kau di n+ya zhes bgyi/ bdag gi ming ni mo 'gal zhes bgyi ste/ bdag de las skyes pa s+ya na/ de'i slad du/ 
12a7(tog gzungs): bdag gi ming ni mo 'gol gyi bu zhes btags so// bdag rab tu byung bar yang pha mas gnang lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis shA ri'i bu dang / mo 'gal gyi bu / 
12b1(tog gzungs): thad du g.yog dang bcas te/ tshangs par spyad pa spyod cig ces bka' bsngal pa dang / de nyid kyis de gnyis rab tu byung ba dang / bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i dge slong gi dngos
12b2(tog gzungs): por to// shA ri'i bu dang / mo 'gal gyi bu g.yog dang bcas pa rab tu byung nas ring po ma ldon par bdud sdig can dbang phyug chen po'i gzugs su/ bcom ldan 'dra
12b3(tog gzungs): kyi spyan sngor 'dug nas 'di skad ces smras so// gang dag bstan btsos don spyod mkhas rig pa'i pha rol song // de kun de yi rkang la phyag 'tshal de dag 'dren pa nga/ 
12b4(tog gzungs): kr-i ta ma slob ma mkhas bcas nga la deng myur skyabs/ tshol cig/ mya ngan 'das 'gro rgyal/ nye ba'i gastsal ba'i lam ni khyod la bshad/ bcom ldan 'das
12b5(tog gzungs): kyis bka' bskul pa/ khyod lam 'gro ba 'di da ga dran 'gror 'dren cing sdug bsnga la rgya mtsho bar byed/ nga yoM lam ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i 'gro ba'i sgra/ 
12b6(tog gzungs): bsngal rgya mtsho skye mas byed pa// 'chal pa 'dzem pa med cing mu tser smra ba lnga skad du yang ci zhig zer/ khyod ni bcom zan bdud kyi las kyis dral du yang 'dir ni
12b7(tog gzungs): byed mi nus/ de nas bdud sdig can gyis dbang phyug chen po'i gzugs me snang bar byas nas/ tshangs pa'i cha byad du bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'dug ste/ 
13a1(tog gzungs): 'di skad ces smras so// khyod kyi shes rab kyis ni las dang nyon mongs srid pa'i myu gu rab tu bsal/ de la yi spyan chad thub pa ci 'dra sems can
13a2(tog gzungs): don 'dir 'di ltar sdug bsngal spro/ gtso bo 'gro ba 'di ni khyod kyi snod 'gyur skye bo gang yang ma mchis ti/ dus 'di lags na skyon dang bral khyod ci yi skad du mu
13a3(tog gzungs): ngan slong mi 'da'/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' bskul pa/ ngas 'dul gang 'khod sems can mtshungs mchis te// dus ni skyon dang bral khyod ci yi slad du med gang+gA'i
13a4(tog gzungs): bye ma snyed/ ngas mthong byer gang yis snying rjes tharabya ba'i ni/ 'gro ba rab 'bring ngan pa degyur pa thar te mthar thug na/ de nas mya ngan 'dra' yis
13a5(tog gzungs): blo gros dran pa g.yos ci bskul// de nas yang bdud sdig can sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde nas yid tshul bcags te/ de nyid du mi snang bar gyur nas rang gi gnas
13a6(tog gzungs): su song ste/ mya ngan gyis khang par zhugs te 'dug pa dang / de'i mod la bdud kyi gnas na 'khod pa'i sems can kun phan tshun 'di skad du ni ci'i rgyus bdag cag gi
13a7(tog gzungs): rgyal po chen po 'di mya ngan gyi khang par zhugs te 'dug pa yang mi shes so zhes 'dri'o// de nas bdud kyi bu mo lnga rgya tsam rab tu dga' bar bya ba'i me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos
13b1(tog gzungs): byeng bya thogs te/ rab tu yid du 'ong ba'i gos dang / lngab lhub kyis bdag cag brgyan nas/ rab tu yid du 'ong zhing mos par byed pa'i lha'i sil snyan byas rab tu
13b2(tog gzungs): yid du 'ong ba'i dbyings kyis glu len gar byed cing yan lag lnga dang ldan pa'i lha'i sil snyan dgra byas nas dga' ba'i rtsed mo dang ldan par bdud sdig can gyi 'dun
13b3(tog gzungs): du 'khod po dang / bdud sdig ce ni des lag pa gnyis bsgrengs nas bos te/ sgra ma byed sgra ma byed ces de skad ces smras pa dang / yud tsam zhig lha'i bu mo dag cang mi
13b4(tog gzungs): zer ba ri 'khod do/ yang glu rab tu blangs shing sil swa/ nan dag byas pa dang / bdud sdig can gyi/ dalag pa gnyis g.yabs te bos so// lha'i bu mo de dag gis
13b5(tog gzungs): dga' ba dang ldan pa'i glu dang / gar dang / sil snyanalan bdun gyi bar du byas pa dang / yang kyade bzhin du bdud sdig can de lag pa bsgrengs nas 'ad cing sgra
13b6(tog gzungs): ma byed sgra ma byed ces zerare ro/ de skad ces smras pa dang / lnga'i bu mo de dag cang mi zer bar 'khod do// de nas lha'i bu mo dbyangs snyun klog ces bya bas bdud sdig can ga la
13b7(tog gzungs): de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btang nas 'di skad ces smras so// gtso bo khyod kyis deng 'dir shi 'phos ltas shig gzigs sam ci/ 'on tam ci zhig de ring 'gro ba zhugs
14a1(tog gzungs): kyis 'khrugs gyur tam/ 'on te 'di na khyod dgra stobs chen 'ga' zhig mchis lags sam/ ci yi slad du khyod ni dwagyes par mi bzhugs thugs ngan
14a2(tog gzungs): mdzad/ bdud kyis smras pa/ nga la dgra yod pa ni stobs ldan sems thul ba/ sa sbrengs shAkya'i bu po sgyu ma bslabs po'i blo/ de ni ci nas gal te rlag par ma gyur na/ 
14a3(tog gzungs): de yis dA yi 'dod khrims 'di ni stongs par byed// lha'i bu mo des smras pa/ gtso bo sringad gsum bcings srid rgya mtsho mtha' rings la/ zad bgyid nus pa'i stobs
14a4(tog gzungs): dang ldan pa su zhig mchis/ bdag po thabs stobs brtson 'grus rtsal rnams gang gis kyang // / de la de ring ma rungs / bgyid par nus ma mchis// bdun
14a5(tog gzungs): kyis smras pa/ sbyin dang brtul zhugs bsam pa smon lam snying rje'i zhabs pa can/ stong pa mtshan ma med pa'i mtshon cha mchog dang gzhu thogs te/ 'khor ba las
14a6(tog gzungs): 'byung rab tu zhi ba'i lam dang 'thun gyur nas/ srid pa ma lus bzlog pa nye bar ston pa byed papo// de'i slob ma bsam btan la ni mngon par brtson yid kyis/ 
14a7(tog gzungs): par rgyu zhing nyis par bya phyir khe zug tu/ cho ga bzhin du zhugs nas grong dang grong khyer stong pa dang / nags kyi nang ngag dang ni ri yi sman ljongs rnams nag na// 
14b1(tog gzungs): rdzu 'phrul dang ni stobs dang snying rje'i grogs dang ldan pa yi/ dam pa nye rgyal pang nas skyes gnyis thub pas btul bar 'gyur/ rab btul chos las 'jig rten gsum
14b2(tog gzungs): du tshe ge bzhin du btul/ des ni nga yi 'dod khams 'di dag stongs par byed par 'gyur/ de nas bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya po de dag gis/ bdud sdig can las/ bcom ldan
14b3(tog gzungs): 'dus kyi yon tan dang sngags pa thos nas/ thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin rnam pa dang bral ba'i klog ces bya ba thob po/ de nas bdud kyi
14b4(tog gzungs): bu mo lnga rgya bo de dag gis bcom ldan 'das la mcho pa bya ba'i phyir lha'i sil snyan dang / lha'i me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa
14b5(tog gzungs): dang/ lnga lhub dang srung bya dang / rgyan de dag bye com ldan 'das gral bya de logs su gtor ba dang / lha'i me tog drang / sil snyan nas rgyan gyi bar de dag rtsa
14b6(tog gzungs): ljon 'das kyi rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus/ 'od mo'i tshal du bas par gyur to// bdud kyi bu mo de drug kyang g.yog dang bcas pas/ so so nAs bcom ldan 'das mthong ngo // 
14b7(tog gzungs): de dag gis mthong nas kyang rab tu dga' ba dang / rangs pa skyes par gyur to// gang gis phyir 'od ma'i tshal du 'di lta bu'i me tog gi char rab tu 'bab ces/ dge slong de dag
17a1(tog gzungs): tsom skyes nas/ bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das shA ri'i bu dang / me'u 'bral gyi bu g.yog dang bcas pa 'di gnyis la/ ngo mtshar rmad du byung
17a2(tog gzungs): ba chen po sngon ma mthong mthos pa'i me tog gi char chen po rab tu 'bab pa legs sam/ bcom ldan 'das 'di'i rgyu ci legs/ rkyen ci lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' ste
17a3(tog gzungs): pa/ rigs kyi bu 'di gnyis kyi mthu ma yin te/ bdud sdig can gyi g.yog mo lnga brgya tsam gyis bdud kyi khang pa de nas nga la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir 'di lta bu'i me tog gi char chen pon
17a4(tog gzungs): rgyan gyi bar gyi char dab po// de nas ring po mi thogs pa kye 'dir 'ongs te/ nga lus bla na med pa yang dgapar rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bstan pa thob po// de nas
17a5(tog gzungs): bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya tsam po de dag so so nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung dang brjod pa'i dbyangs thos nas/ bcom ldan 'das lA de bas kyang rab tu dga' ba skyes te/ de
17a6(tog gzungs): dge dga' mgu rangs pa des byang chub kyi sems mi brjed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob po// de nas yang bdud kyi bu mo de dag bdud kyi khang po der bla gros phrag po gcig
17a7(tog gzungs): tu dgos te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lhang sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das phyogs gang na bzhugs pa'i phyogs der bltas te 'di skad ces gsol to// srid
17b1(tog gzungs): chu ma lus skyems pa 'gro ba'i mig gcig pa/ mig ma mchis pa'i 'jig rten kun la gzigs nas ni/ khyod kyis lha dang mir bcas pa yi 'gro ba sgrol/ thub pa bdag cag ji ltar
17b2(tog gzungs): myur du sangs rgyas 'gyur/ lha dang mis mchod don dam gsung ba bcom ldan 'das/ bdag cag 'thun par bud med skud pa nyid spangs nas// blo mchog khyod kyi 'phrul
17b3(tog gzungs): drung du myur bar ni/ mchis nas 'di bzhin thub pa'i dbang po'i gsung nyid nyan to// bdag med gsung ba don dam gzigs pa bcom ldan 'das// byang chub yan lag rin
17b4(tog gzungs): chen dri med nor gsung sgron/ mtshungs med bdud kyi stong btul khyod kyis bdag cag la// de ltar myur/ du lhan cig byang chub lung bstan gsol/ de nas bdud
17b5(tog gzungs): kyi bu mo de dag stan las langasra te mgrin gcig tu bdud sdig tsun la 'di skad ces smras so// nyes byas blo gros can khyod snying po med g.yo ba'i/ dpal rnyed ci phyir bcom ldan
17b6(tog gzungs): 'das la sdang bar sems/ dregs pas gos nas skye ba la sogs sdug bsngal gyis// lus kun gtses te mi bzad gnas su nye song / de ltar khre'u ba spangs te rgyal la dad
17b7(tog gzungs): par gyis/ 'khor ba'i nyes pa dregs pa'i 'dam las thar pa'i bdag/ 'di ni kyis 'gro ba kun gyi ngo bo mkhyen/ thugs rje can gyi skyabs su 'dong gis myur du bzhud/ de nA
18a1(tog gzungs): bdud sdig can shin du gdug pa'i yid dang ldan pas 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis 'di 'dra'i bdud kyi stobs kyi yul drag po dran par byas pa/ gang
18a2(tog gzungs): g.yog mo lnga brgya tsamu 'di dgra bdag nyid bcing ba lngas bcings par mthong bar byas te/ 'di las bzlog lA 'gro mi nus par bya'o// snyam pa dang khadu des de dag
18a3(tog gzungs): bcing ma nus so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar g.yog mo lnga brgya tsam po de dag de bzhin gshegs pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i phyir ro// de nas g.yog mo lnga brgya po
18a4(tog gzungs): de dag bdud sdig can gyis drung nas dong ba dang / de nas bdud sdig can rab tu khros te 'di snyam/ du sems so// bdag gis yang 'di 'dra ba'i bdud kyi yul
18a5(tog gzungs): po dran par byas te/ ci nas bdag gi g.yog mo de gi phyogs dang phyogs 'tshams thams cad 'khrul nas/ dge sbyong kau ta ma mi mthong zhing slararA yang bdag gi gnas su 'ong
18a6(tog gzungs): bar na mkha' 'di dag thams cad rnam par 'thor rlung dang / rlung nag po chen po chen pos kun du khyab par bya'o snyam nas yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis rlung cud
18a7(tog gzungs): zad kyang langs par byed ma nus so// tha na skra'i rtse mo gcig tsam yang bskyod par ma nus na/ mang du lta ci smos/ de nas yang bdud sdig can rab tu khros shing sdug bsngal
18b1(tog gzungs): te yid la bcags nas/ ngu zhing skad chen pos rang gi bu dang tshogs kyi 'khor la bos te/ bdud kyi gnas thams cad sgras gang bar byas so// bsdug pa'i bu dang tshogs kyi
18b2(tog gzungs): 'khor rnams tshur shog shig/ nga ni bdagra yul rang gi rdzu 'phrul stobs las nyams/ shAkya'i bu 'di sgyu ldan g.yon can ngag 'dzam la/ khong nas rang bzhin sdong 'dra
18b3(tog gzungs): ba 'dir skyes so// de nas sgra des bdud kyi g.yog mo dang / bdud kyi bu mo de dag thams nA di dang bdud kyi bu tshogs dang byas pa thams cad rings pa'i gzugs kyis myur du
18b4(tog gzungs): ljags nas/ bdug sdig can gyis mdun du 'khod// ste 'khor de'i nang nas bdud kyi bu rgyal ba'o/ blo gros zhes bya ba des thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras/ 
18b5(tog gzungs): ci'i slad du thugs khros rab tu 'khrugs shing thugs ma dges/ bsreg bskal deng 'dir ma byung 'di nas khyod ma 'phos/ 'di na khyod lhag dgra nI su yang ma mchis
18b6(tog gzungs): na/ khyod ni rmongs par gyur tam ci slad gzhan du dgongs/ bdud kyis smras pa/ shAkya'i bu pho dmangs phal shing gi grib mar 'dug pa ma mthong ngam// ci phyir 'di na
18b7(tog gzungs): khyod kyi mdun na stobs dang ldan pa'i dgra med smras// stobs cig ldan pa g.yon can de yis thams cad rnam pa du mar bslus/ bdag cag bu dang sder bcas me lce 'bar dang
19a1(tog gzungs): bcas pa me yis bsregs/ 'jig rten 'di na skyes bu gtso bo dpral dang brjod pa rnam grags pa/ mukhris pa bstan bcos snya mngags mang po byed brtson 'thun
19a2(tog gzungs): par myur bar yang // chos kyi ko ba btang gis drangs te shAkya'i bu 'di'i di ring bskye bas dang spong / lus mdzes g.yon can blo gros ldan 'di nga yi dgror ni rab tu gnas
19a3(tog gzungs): rab tu sdug pa'i g.yog mo de dag snying rje med pas ngabar te/ nga la dbang btsugs nas ni dge sbyong de yi bskyabs su song / gal te bdag cag myur bsgribs
19a4(tog gzungs): stobs chen 'di deng thal bar ma byas na// g.yo dang sgyu yis srid pa gsum po de dag ma lus stongs par byed/ de nas bdud kyi bu tshogs kyi 'khor dang / 
19a5(tog gzungs): bcas pa de dag thams cad kyis thal mo sbyar te 'di skad ces smras so// de ltar bgyi'o// bdag cag gi rdzu 'phrul dang stobs kyi yul gyi mthu dang rnam par
19a6(tog gzungs): 'brul pa de thams cad bstan te/ shAkya'i bu 'di gal te thul bar 'gyid nus pa ldan ni legs/ de ltar ma nus na ni de'i bskyabs su mchi'o// yang nyid mngon sum
19a7(tog gzungs): du gyur pa lags te/ gang bdag cag sde chen pos yongs su bskor ba sngar shAkya'i bu gcig pu gnyis su med par 'dis rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs kyis rab tu pham par bgyis
19b1(tog gzungs): ma/ de g.yog mang por gyur pa lta ci spos/ bdud sdig can gyis smras pa/ bzhin bzangs dag deng la gal te dge sbyong kr-i ta ma 'di gsod nus na sngar sheg shig/ ci stem
19b2(tog gzungs): nus na yang bdag cag gli gnas kyang bsrung gis sker sheg shig/ de nas bdud kyi 'khor dkrigs blag bcu gnyi sde po de dag de nas 'phags te/ 'di nas steng du dpa
19b3(tog gzungs): tshad brgyad khri bzhi stong gi bar du bkang nas de 'dra ba'i bdud kyi stobs kyi yul gyi rdzu 'phrul drag po bstan te/ gang gling bzhi pa'i nam mkha' thams cad rab du sprin nag po thang
19b4(tog gzungs): dang / rlung nag po chen po dang / skar madrangs kang ba nas ri'i rgyal po ri rab la yat+pa lag gis brdabs te/ gling byizhi pa thams cad rab tu g.yo bar byas nas/ shin du
19b5(tog gzungs): 'jigs pa'i sgra rnams kyang 'byin to// de dag gi klu dang / klu chen po dang / gnod sbyin dang / gnod sbyin chen po de dag gis sa chen po brag dang rir bcas pa thaM da
19b6(tog gzungs): dang ldan pa dang / ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyang g.yos par rig/ ga mtsho dang mtsho chen po dang / 'bab chu dang chu phrin dang 'bab chu chen po dang / mtsho chen po rnams kyang 'khrugs par
19b7(tog gzungs): rig nas/ na mkha'i dkyil 'khor na 'khod do// bdud kyi 'khor de dag ni ri rab kyi zom la 'khod nas/ dpag tshad tsam gyi rdo'i char mngon par sprul te/ na mkha' las kun du
20a1(tog gzungs): 'bebs so// ral gri dang / gtun shing dang / rdo dang mtshon rtse gnyis pa dang / ste'u ka ma la dang / lcags mda' dang / spu gri lta bu dang / dgra sta dang / ste'u song// 
20a2(tog gzungs): bu dang / khwa rang rod can dang / shin du kha rang rod can dang / sra ba drag pa rtsub pa/ rno ba'i char rab tu sprul te/ kun du phab bo// de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das bdud kyi 'khor
20a3(tog gzungs): rnams par 'jig pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ ga rno ba dang / mtshon de dag thams cad lha'i me tog ut+pal dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu ta dang
20a4(tog gzungs): dkar po dang / man+ta ra ba dang / man+dA ra ba chen po dang / me tog gi char chen por byin gyis brlabs/ yul ang+ga mang+ga d+he rme/ mnga' ldang ba ni spos kyi char chen
20a5(tog gzungs): por byin gyis brlabs te/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi sgra dang / chos kyi sgra dang / dge 'dun gyi sgra dang / pha rol du phyin pa'i sgra dang / mngon par 'du shes pa'i
20a6(tog gzungs): sgra dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i sgra dang / dbang bskur ba'i sgra dang / bdud bzhi pham par byas pa'i sgra dang / byang chub kyi snying por 'gro ba'i sgra dang / len pa dang bcas pa'i
20a7(tog gzungs): sgra dang / len pa med pa'i sgrar byin gyis brlabs/ rdul dang mun nag dang / rlung thams cad kyang rab tu zhi ba'o// gang gling bzhi pa 'di na/ rtsa dang / shing rgol ba dang / sman
20b1(tog gzungs): dang nags tshal dang / sa dang blag dang 'i ci yod pa de dag thams cad ni rin po che sna bdun du byin gyis brlab so// bcom ldan 'das gtsug tor ltar mi mthong bya dang / 
20b2(tog gzungs): ldan pa'i tshangs pa'i 'jig rten gyi bar du skus dbang mdzad do// bcom ldan 'das kyi mtshan re re las kyang 'di 'dra ba'i 'od byung ste/ 'od des stong gsum gyi stong chen
20b3(tog gzungs): po'i 'jig rten gyi khams snang ba chen pos khyab par gyur to// stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten bya khams 'di'i lha dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma

35a3(tog gzungs): bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di bshad ma thag tu yang sa chen po g.yos so// bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya tsam mo de dag kyang rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di

2a8(tog gzungs kha 3): mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pas bcom ldan 'das cang mi gsung bar rig nas/ de nyid du mi snang bar 'gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' bstsal pa/

6a3(tog gzungs kha 4): mtshan rnams/ bsrung ba byed de tsa the tsom med// brgya byin lha de de bac+doMs po dang / tshungs pa khyab 'jug dbang chen dang / dga' ba'i dbang po nag po che/ smin drug bu dang tshogs
6a4(tog gzungs kha 4): kyi dbang / me mo'i tshigs rnams thams cad dang / de bzhin bdun ris gzhan rnams dang / drang srong gzi brjid cha rnams dang / rdzu 'phrul chen po'i lha rnams dang / de kun
6a5(tog gzungs kha 4): skye so 'brang ma'i gzungs 'dzin de la bsrung byed 'gyur// sangs rgyas bdag nyid che rnams dang // rig pa'i lha mi stobs chen dang / bdag gi ma dang khri gnyer dang / lha mo
6a6(tog gzungs kha 4): sgrol ma lcags kyu dang / rdo rje lug gu rgyud dang dka ra~M/ de bzhin dkar mo chen po dang / nage mo che dang po nya dang / de bzhin rdo rje po nya gzhan/ zhugs pa bzang dang rdo rje zhags// 
6a7(tog gzungs kha 4): lan nas rdo rje stobs po che rin po rig pa chen me rdo rje 'phyang / bdud rtsi thal sbyor byed pa dang // gzhan gyis mi thob lha mo che// rna ba nag mo stobs chen mo// dpal yod ldan pa/ 
6b1(tog gzungs kha 4): bskal chen dang / rnan gdung 'khor bad+ma 'dra/ me tog so can nor bu btsug/ sgra mdog mdzes dang khyam pa mo// lha mo gzi brjid chen mo dang / dpal yon ldan pa klos/ 
6b2(tog gzungs kha 4): 'phreng can// srin mo ral pa gcig pa dang / sangs rgyas srungs zhes pa dang / bskal pa chen po'i mi thod can// lang ga'i bdag mo dpal yod can/ gzhan yang lnga
6b3(tog gzungs kha 4): mo mang po rnams/ sems can rjes su 'dzin byed dag/ rig pa gang gi lag na gnas/ de la srung byed par 'gyur/ 'phrog ma dang ni lngas rtsen dang // dung can dang ni so can/ 
6b4(tog gzungs kha 4): ma/ dpal gyi lha mo dbyangs can yang // de'i rjes su 'gro rtag tu srung // so so 'brang ma'i chen mo 'di// bud med gang zhig rtag chang na/ de'i thams cad grub par 'gyur/ 
6b5(tog gzungs kha 4): rtag par mngal du bu po chags/ mngal rnams na yang bde bar skye/ sgyum ma dag kyang bde bar 'gyur/ nad dang sdig pa thams cad kyang 'jig par 'gyur// the tsom med// 
6b6(tog gzungs kha 4): bsod nams ldan zhing stobs dang ldan/ nir dang 'bru yang rtag tu 'phel/ tshig kyang gzungs par 'os pa dang / mchod pa'i 'os su gyur pa yin/ bud med dang / ni skyes
6b7(tog gzungs kha 4): pa'ang rur/ rtsang ma gang zhing 'chang sel ni/ de ni sems can thams cad dag/ thar par du phyir brtson par 'gyur/ rtag tu byed par 'gyur ba yin/ nad to cog kyang rnam par spang
7a1(tog gzungs kha 4): sras dang skye bo mang btsas pa'i/ rgyal po 'dra de'i dbang du 'gyur// phun sum tshogs pa rtag tu 'byung // bsod nams phung po rnams par 'phel/ de ni bsam pa
7a2(tog gzungs kha 4): thams cad grub/ dkyil 'khor kun du zhugs pa yin/ rnams kyi bka' bo nan du/ de ni kun du dam tshig shes// rmi la mngon pa rmi lam mi 'gyur/ sdig pa thams
7a3(tog gzungs kha 4): cad 'phrog pa'i mchog/ sdig pa rnams dang de bzhin du/ dgra yang rab tu bung bar byed/ gza' kun rnam par gzhi'i phyir/ ye shes chen po dbang phyug chen po gsungs
7a4(tog gzungs kha 4): 'dod pa thams cad sbyin par byed/ de phyir rtag tu bcang bar bya/ 'byung po'i tshogs rnams ngal nyon/ da ni bar tu 'di brjod do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag
7a5(tog gzungs kha 4): 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / sangs rgyas dang chos dang ches dang dge bdun la phyag 'tshal lo// / oM byi bu la gAr+b+he/ byi bu
7a6(tog gzungs kha 4): la bi mA la/ dza sa gar+b+he/ badz+ra dza la gain+d+he/ gartig ha ne/ gar+b+he gag ni bai sho d+ha ni/ sarba pa bA bi sho d+ha ne/ oM kun baT+wAMg ga nI bi tsI'i ni/ tsa le ga ge ri ni/ gi rig no/

7b1(tog gzungs kha 4): gu ru gu ru gu ru ni/ tsa le tsu lu tsi ri ni/ mu tsi le dza ya bi tsa ye/ sarba b+ha ya bi gi ti/ garba ma ba ra ni/ si ri si ri/ mi ri mi ri/ g+hi ri g+hi ri/ bi ri bi ri/ bcom ldan 'das ma
7b2(tog gzungs kha 4): sems can 'dren ma/ kun nas 'dren ma/ 'gra thams cad 'joms ma bdag 'jigs pa thams cad dang / ngan log pa thams cad dang / nad thams cad las bsrung
7b3(tog gzungs kha 4): du gsol/ bsrung du gsol// tsi ri tsi ri/ bi ri bi ri/ kI ri ki ri/ b+hi ri b+hi ri/ b+hi b+hi d+hi/ a pa ran/ bi shod d+ha ni/ mu ri mu ri/ tsi li tsi li/ ka ma le/ bi ma le/ dza yau dza/ 
7b4(tog gzungs kha 4): yai/ ba he dza ya/ ba ti/ bcom ldan 'das ma rin po che'i cod pan dang 'dren 'phreng ba mnga' ba/ cha byad rnam pa sna tshogs mda' na bcom ldan 'das ma rig pa'i lha mo sdig pa'i
7b5(tog gzungs kha 4): las thams cad rnam par spyod pa/ bdag thams cad du kun nas bsrung du gsol/ bsrung du gsol// hu ru hu ru/ 'gon ma mchis pa skyabasu ma mchis pa/ dpung gnye
7b6(tog gzungs kha 4): mchis pa bsrung du gsol/ ba dag sdug bsngal thams cad las thar par mdzad du gsol/ tsan dI tsan de tse na da ni/ be gre ba ni/ su du g+ta ti ni pa'i ni/ mun tra pa krA mi b+h+re/ 
7b7(tog gzungs kha 4): ra na bra ma tha ni/ badzi yang b+ha hi ni/ hu ri d+hu ru/ mu ru mu ru/ tsu ru tsu ru/ a gu bal ni/ su pra bar ma tha ni/ sarba de pa ta pu'u dzi te/ d+hi ra d+hi ri/ saM man tra a la gyi te/ khrem blo br-imar+g+ha
8a1(tog gzungs kha 4): ka te/ su pra ba b+ha bi shu te/ sarba pa pa bi sho d+ha ni/ d+ha ra d+ha ra d+ha ra d+ha ni/ bA ra d+ha ne/ tsA le tsa le/ su mu su mu/ su mu su mu su mu ru/ ru ru tsA le/ tsa le tsa le/ dpral gyi sku mangs
8a2(tog gzungs kha 4): ba bdag la gnod par pa sems can pa las bskyabs du gsol/ bdag gi bsam pa rdzogs par mdzad du gi so la// dzaM ye ke mai l-i/ krA ni kru ni/ pa ra di ang gu she/ oM pad ma byi
8a3(tog gzungs kha 4): shud d+hA/ sho d+ha ya sho d+ha yaM/ shud d+ha shud d+he b+ha/ raM b+ha ra/ b+hi ri b+hi ri/ b+hu ru b+hu ru/ mang ga la bi shud d+he/ pa bid dra mu khyaM/ khang gyi ni khad gyi ni/ khA ra kha ra/ dzo li ti shi kha re/ sa man
8a4(tog gzungs kha 4): ti pra so ri ta/ a ba b+ha si da shud di/ dz+wa la dz+wa la/ sarba de ba gnA/ gA ha na/ kr-i tA sa ma ka ra sha ni/ sAd t+yA pra te/ ta ra ti raM/ glang po che'i lha stangs kyis gzungs ma/ bdag bsgral du
8a5(tog gzungs kha 4): gsol// hu lu hu lu/ hu tu hUM tu/ kI ni kr-i naM/ bi shi bi shi/ g+hi ni g+he ni/ ha na ni ha nA ni/ sarba gra ha b+hi kra ni/ pang ga li tsu mu tsu mu/ su mu su mu/ su pi tsa la/ ta rA ta ra// bcom
8a6(tog gzungs kha 4): ldan 'das ma blong po che'i lci stengs kyis gzungs ma/ thams cad du kun nas phyogs thams cad du du bcing ba dang / rdo rje'i rab dang / rdo rje zhags pas bcings pas/ bdag
8a7(tog gzungs kha 4): 'jigs pa chen po brgyad las bsgral du gsil// badz+ra dz+wa la byi shud d+hi/ kar kar/ d+hu ri b+hu ri/ bag po ti/ gzapa ti/ ga b+ha 'i she d+ha ni/ ku k+kis du'u ri ni/ dza la dza la
8b1(tog gzungs kha 4): gtsa la/ dza la ni/ lha'i chos kun du char dbub du gsol/ a mri ti bar sha ni/ de pa ta a pa ri ni/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rabs bdud rtsi'i mchog dang ldan pa bdag la
8b2(tog gzungs kha 4): dbang bskur du gsel// 'thab pa dang 'thab mo dang / rtsod pa dang 'gyed pa dang / rmi lam ngan pa dang / kra mi shis pa dang / sdig pa thams cad rnam par sbyong ba/ gnon sbyin dang srin
8b3(tog gzungs kha 4): po dang / klu thams dang 'joms pa/ gnon pas 'jigs skrag pa/ bdag 'jigs thams cad dang / gnon thams cad nad 'go ba thams cad dang / nad thams cad las
8b4(tog gzungs kha 4): thams ca rtag par srung du gsol/ bsrung du gsol/ bya la ba la/ nga la ti/ dza ma dza la/ thams cad du dus kun nas bdag la rgyal ba mdzad du gsol/ bdag la rig
8b5(tog gzungs kha 4): chen mo 'di grub par mdzad du gsol/ dkyil 'khor chen po 'di bsgrub du gsol/ gsang sngags rnams bsgrub tu gsol// dbyugs rnams gzhom du gsol// dza ma dza ya/ sing
8b6(tog gzungs kha 4): dwe sid d+he/ sid d+he sid d+he/ dud d+ha bud d+ha/ 'du bu ra ya 'bu bu ra ya/ bai'u rini bu'u ni/ bdag gi bsam pa rdzogs par mdzad du gsol// rig pa thams cad las byung ba la sku can/ 
8b7(tog gzungs kha 4): rgyal ba lhag par rgyal ba can/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po rnam par bdag pa bcom ldan 'das ma bzhugs su gsol// bzhugasu gsol// dam tshig skyong du gsol// 'jigs
8b8(tog gzungs kha 4): pa mi bzed pa chen po brgyad las bdag la gzigasu gsol/ sarba a pa ra ni bi shod ni/ sa ra sa ra/ pra sa ra pra sar/ sarba a par nab sho da ni sa man ta/ a ka ra man d+ha la bi gud
9a1(tog gzungs kha 4): d+he/ bi ki te bi ka ti/ bi ga te mA le/ sarba ma la bi sho d+ha na/ kri ni kli ni/ sarba pa la bi shud de/ bral big te/ te dze te tsa ba te/ badz+ra badz+ra pa ti/ 'jig rten gsum du byin gyis brlabs pa la swA hA/ 
9a2(tog gzungs kha 4): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis spyi bo nas dbang bskur ba la swAhA/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis dbang skur ba le sahUM/ lha thams cad kyis de bong bskur ba la sahA/ de bzhin
9a3(tog gzungs kha 4): gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying pos byin brlabs pa las / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig grub pa las hU~M/ dbang po dang che ba'i dbang po dang ldan pa dbang pos rnams par smras/ 
9a4(tog gzungs kha 4): pa la swAhA/ tshangs pa dang tshangs pa gnas pa la swA hA/ khyab 'jug gyis phyag byas pa la swA hA/ dbang phyug chen pos phyag 'tshal cing mchod pa la swAhA/ rdo rje 'chang lag na rdo rje'i stobs dang / brtson
9a5(tog gzungs kha 4): 'grus kyi byin b+harlabs pA la swA hA/ yul 'khor srung la swA hA/ 'phags skyes po la swAhA/ mi bzang l-i sahA/ rnam thos kyi bu la swAhA/ rgyal po chen po bzhis phyag byas pa la sahA/ gshin rjel/ 
9a6(tog gzungs kha 4): sad+g+ha/ ga~M shi rjes mchod cing drug byas pa la sar+b+ba/ tshwa lA la s+ye/ rA lnga chen po las d+ha/ me lha lu swAtwA/ klu'i rnam par bltas pA li swA hA/ lnga'i tshogs rnam pa la swAt+ma/ klu'i tsho gas rnams pa
9a7(tog gzungs kha 4): la swAhA/ gnod sbyin gyi tshogs rnams pa la si h+ye/ srin po'i tshogs rnams pa la swAhA/ dri zla'i tshogs rnams la suh+ma/ lha ma yin gyi tshogs rnams la sam+b+ha/ na mkha'i lding gi tshogs rnams la/ 
9a8(tog gzungs kha 4): swA hA/ mi 'am ci'i tshogs rnams la swA hA/ lto 'phye chen po'i tshogs rnam la sa hUM/ mi rnams la swA hA/ mi me yin pa rnams la swA hA/ gdon thams cad la swA hA/ 'byung po thams
9b1(tog gzungs kha 4): cad la swAhA/ yi dgas la sahA/ sha za la swAhA/ brjed byed la sahA/ gnod po la swAhA/ grul bum la swA hA/ oM d+hA ru d+hA ru swA hA/ tu ru tu ru sahA/ mu ru mu ru/ swAhA/ ha na ha na sarba sha
9b2(tog gzungs kha 4): hwa'un sa hUM/ da ha da hA sarba duSh+TA nAn swA hA/ pa tsa pa tsa sarba pA t+ye rI ka pra t+ya mi drin sru hrI/ gang dag bdag le mi phan pa ri 'ded pe de bdag thams cad kyi lus/ dza la ya sArba tsi duSh+Ta cing
9b3(tog gzungs kha 4): tan na swA he/ 'bar ba la swA hA/ rab tu 'bar ba sahA/ rdo rje 'bar ba la swAhA/ me lce 'bar ba la swAhA/ kun du 'bar ba la swAhA/ nor bu bzang l-i swA hA/ gang ba bzang po la sahA/ 
9b4(tog gzungs kha 4): nag ni po chen po la swA hA/ ma mo'i tshogs la sa ha/ gnod sbyin mo rnams la sahA/ srin mo rnams la sahA/ na mkha'i ma mo rnams la swA hA/ brgya mtshon gnas rnams la swA hA/

9b6(tog gzungs kha 4): la swAhA/ zas su mngal za ba rnams la sa hA/ mngal 'dzin pa rnams la sah+la/ hu lu phu lA sihUM/ oM swA s+sas swAhA/ b+h+r-i ba sUh+na/ b+hU bA seswa b+hai'u ra bA s+yAhA/ b+h+r-i 'u ra
9b7(tog gzungs kha 4): swA hU~M/ tsau ti tsi ti sa hA/ bi ti bi ti swA hA/ ha d+hA ra ni swAhA/ d+ha ri ni swA hUM/ oM ga~M ni swA hA/ te tse bu ba swA hUM/ tsi li tsi li/ sad+d+haM/ mi li mi l+r-i/ swAhA/

10a1(tog gzungs kha 4): b+ha ya dza b+ha ya sAd+d+ha/ sra swam b+ha ya s+thAm b+hA ya sAhA/ tshin d+hA tshin d+ha swAh+ma b+hin d+ha b+hin d+ha/ swAh+ma/ b+han dza b+hA na dza swAhA/ b+hAn d+ha b+hAn d+ha/ mo ha ya mo ha ya swAg+na/ ma ni bi shud+d+he
10a2(tog gzungs kha 4): swA hA/ su'u r+ya swA hA/ su'u r+ya b+ho shud d+he swA hA/ bi sho d+ha ni soh+ma/ tsan tre tsan tre ba ni b+hu'u rnA tsa na tre swA hA/ gre tre byo swA hA/ na ge kan tre b+h+yAM swA hA/ shi be bya swA hA/ shin ti swA hA/ puSh+paM swA hA/ swa sta ye

10b7(tog gzungs kha 4): bag med pa'i dbang gi sa ma cings pas/ de khros nas de la bzung ba dang / de tshor ba mi bzod pa myong nas/ ji ltar yang dag par ni srog dang bral lo snyam du shes so// de

11a5(tog gzungs kha 4): grang su chud pa zhig/ grong khyer chen po ba ra na se na sngon yongasu rgyu ba'i tshe/ de'i shar phyogs kyi stobs kyis 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po des/ dpung gi tshogs go dgos te/

11a7(tog gzungs kha 4): grong khyer 'phrog pa la thug na/ thabs gang gis pha rol gyi dmag tshogs de zhim par bgyi bka' stsal du gsol zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal pos khyed 'tsher gri ba chung ngur gyis
11b1(tog gzungs kha 4): shig/ rig pa'i rgyal mo sor 'brang ma chen mo zhes byas yod de/ ngas des dpung gis tshogs yan lag gzhi pa ni pham par byas so// thal ba bzhin du bya'o// zhes sgo ba dang /

11b3(tog gzungs kha 4): de nas rgyal po chen po tshangs pas byin gyis spros chu sna tshoT kyis mgo bkrus te/ gos gtsang ma bgos nas/ rig pa'i rgyal mo 'di cho ga bzhin du bris te/ mgo'i gtsug gi
11b4(tog gzungs kha 4): skra'i nang du bzhag nas rig pa'i rgyal mo 'di nyid kyis go cha byas te g.yul gyi nang du zhugs pa dang / gcig pu'i dpung gi tshogs yan lag bzhi pa thams cad phan par bya ba te
11b5(tog gzungs kha 4): ji srid du skyabs su dong bde srid 'das tshar bcad nas/ stobs kyis 'khor lo sgyur ba de gcig pu btang ngo // bram ze chen po de ltar rig pa'i rgyal po chen mo de bzhin gshegs
11b6(tog gzungs kha 4): pa thams can gyis snying po dang / phyag rgyas byin gyis brlabs pa thu chen po mngon sum du gyur pa yin te/ mngon sum du gyur to// snyam du bzung bar bya'o// de bzhin gshegs

14b1(tog gzungs kha 5): bzhis byung ba gyis pag kyi yang rlung ba'i snang ba de dag gnang na 'di mchog dpa gtso bung pa rab mchog 'grus// rkye nas bcom ldan 'das rgyal blong
14b2(tog gzungs kha 5): bcad de gsol pa/ mi mchog gang zhig mdo 'di dag yongasu rdzogs pas srung ba dag bde legs bgying ba de la ni/ srin po rnams kyang 'chi mi bgyi su yang rung ste mdo di sa
14b3(tog gzungs kha 5): mi mchog gis ni gsungs pa bzhin yong su rdzogs shing ma chad par// shin du tshang bar 'chang bgyid pa/ de la gnod sbyin yi dgas dang / 'byung po grul bum srin po dang / sgra
14b4(tog gzungs kha 5): byed rgyu ba ku rnams dang / de lta bu dag 'tshe mi bgyid// de dag mi ma lags pa'i gnod// myur du gu du 'chi bar 'gyur// de la cis kyang mi tshugs te// de la 'tsho ba yod mi nus/ rgya
14b5(tog gzungs kha 5): po chen po badz+re/ pa yis// bcoM ldan 'das phyag 'tshal zhes brjod do// sangs rgyas nabs la phya ge'i tshol nas/ de nyid du ni mi snang gyur/ nas bcom ldan 'das de'i mtshan mi 'das
14b6(tog gzungs kha 5): te/ nam langs nas dge slong gi dge 'dun gyi gung la bzhugs te/ dge slong rnams la bka' bstsal pa/ dge slong ma dang sum rgyal po chen po bzhi bu dang bcas/ blon po dang bcas 'gro// 
14b7(tog gzungs kha 5): dang bcas/ ma smag gzhug dang bcas/ pho nya dang bcas/ g.yog 'khor dang bcas/ kha dog 'phags pa dag nam sres na lhags nas gros 'thun par dur khrod chen po bsil ba'i cha
